					72 Versetl sammt 12 Toccaten (Muffat, Gottlieb)				</h1>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>12 toccatas &amp; 72 versetti
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1726 - <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://opac.rism.info/metaopac/search?q=rism00000990046456&amp;db=251&amp;View=rism&amp;Language=en">Vienna: F.A. Dietel</a></span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Versets&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Versets</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Toccatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Toccatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_keyboard&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For keyboard</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="6 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_keyboard_soloists&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring keyboard soloists</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_1_player&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 1 player</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_2_trumpets%2C_2_trombones_%28arr%29&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 2 trumpets, 2 trombones (arr)</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_4_players&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 4 players</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_trumpet&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the trumpet</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_trombone&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the trombone</a></span></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Versetl? I know google disagrees with me on this one and has lots of hits for Versetl (oddly, almost all in association with this publication), but shouldn't that be Verseti or, indeed, Versetti? - Schissel
<br />
No. "Versetl" seem to be not an italian but an old (austrian)german name. Even in the first Edition at Muffats Lifetime the name ends on the cover as in the preface everytime it is mentioned clearly not with "i" but with "l". Nevertheless since it is used for very short fugues it could be at least derived from the italian "versetti" in the meaning of very short chapter/paragraph. fahl5
</p>
